   112	class RemoteWorkplanGateway:
   113	    """Reference SQLite remote gateway.
   114	
   115	    ``clock`` returns seconds since epoch (or a :class:`datetime`) and is
   116	    injectable for deterministic expiry tests. Public methods are keyword-only
   117	    except the database path constructor argument.
   118	    """
   119	
   120	    def __init__(self, db_path: str, clock: Callable[[], int | float | datetime] | None = None):
   121	        self.store = SQLiteStore(db_path)
   122	        self._clock = clock or time.time
   123	
   124	    def _now(self) -> int:
   125	        value = self._clock()
   126	        return int(value.timestamp() if isinstance(value, datetime) else value)
   127	
   128	    @staticmethod
   129	    def _credential_hash(credential: str) -> str:
   130	        return hashlib.sha256(credential.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
   131	
   132	    def issue_host_credential(
   133	        self, *, actor: str, scopes: Iterable[str], ttl_seconds: int = 300
   134	    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
   135	        if not actor or actor.count(":") < 2:
   136	            raise GatewayError("invalid_actor", "actor must include namespace, host, and session")
   137	        normalized_scopes = tuple(sorted(set(scopes)))
   138	        if not normalized_scopes or not set(normalized_scopes) <= ALL_SCOPES:
   139	            raise GatewayError("invalid_scope", "credential scopes contain an unsupported action")
   140	        if ttl_seconds <= 0:
   141	            raise GatewayError("invalid_ttl", "credential ttl must be positive")
   142	        now = self._now()
   143	        secret = "rwg_" + secrets.token_urlsafe(32)
   144	        credential_id = str(uuid4())
   145	        with self.store.transaction() as db:
   146	            db.execute(
   147	                "INSERT INTO credentials VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NULL)",
   148	                (credential_id, actor, self._credential_hash(secret), _canonical(normalized_scopes), now, now + ttl_seconds),
   149	            )
   150	        return IssuedCredential(secret, credential_id, actor, normalized_scopes, now + ttl_seconds).to_dict()
   151	
   152	    def revoke_host_credential(self, *, credential: str) -> None:
   153	        with self.store.transaction() as db:
   154	            cursor = db.execute(
   155	                "UPDATE credentials SET revoked_at=? WHERE secret_hash=? AND revoked_at IS NULL",
   156	                (self._now(), self._credential_hash(credential)),
   157	            )
   158	            if cursor.rowcount != 1:
   159	                raise GatewayError("invalid_credential", "credential is unknown or revoked")
   160	
   161	    def _authorize(self, db: sqlite3.Connection, credential: str, scope: str, *, coordinator: bool = False) -> str:
   162	        row = db.execute(
   163	            "SELECT * FROM credentials WHERE secret_hash=?", (self._credential_hash(credential),)
   164	        ).fetchone()
   165	        now = self._now()
   166	        if row is None or row["revoked_at"] is not None:
   167	            raise GatewayError("invalid_credential", "credential is unknown or revoked")
   168	        if row["expires_at"] <= now:
   169	            raise GatewayError("credential_expired", "credential has expired")
   170	        if scope not in json.loads(row["scopes_json"]):
   171	            raise GatewayError("scope_denied", f"credential does not allow {scope}")
   172	        actor = row["actor"]
   173	        if coordinator and not actor.startswith("coordinator:"):
   174	            raise GatewayError("coordinator_required", f"{scope} requires coordinator authority")
   175	        return actor
   176	
   177	    @staticmethod
   178	    def _card(db: sqlite3.Connection, card_id: str) -> sqlite3.Row:
   179	        row = db.execute("SELECT * FROM cards WHERE card_id=?", (card_id,)).fetchone()
   180	        if row is None:
   181	            raise GatewayError("card_not_found", f"card {card_id} does not exist")
   182	        return row
   183	
   184	    @staticmethod
   185	    def _expected(card: sqlite3.Row, expected_revision: int) -> None:
   465	        if (
   466	            binding["repository_id"] != repository_id
   467	            or binding["branch"] != branch
   468	            or binding["base_commit"] != base_commit
   469	            or binding["worktree_path"] != expected["worktreePath"]
   470	            or branch != expected["branch"]
   471	            or base_commit != expected["baseCommit"]
   472	        ):
   473	            raise GatewayError("lineage_mismatch", "repository, worktree, branch, or base commit differs from the frozen definition")
   474	        if (
   475	            set(ancestry) != {"base_commit", "head_commit", "is_descendant", "verification"}
   476	            or ancestry.get("base_commit") != base_commit
   477	            or ancestry.get("head_commit") != head_commit
   478	            or ancestry.get("is_descendant") is not True
   479	            or not isinstance(ancestry.get("verification"), str)
   480	            or not ancestry["verification"]
   481	        ):
   482	            raise GatewayError("invalid_lineage", "head lineage requires structured descendant evidence")
   483	        return binding
   484	
   485	    def claim(
   486	        self, *, card_id: str, expected_revision: int, expected_definition_hash: str,
   487	        credential: str, lease_seconds: int = 120,
   488	    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
   489	        if lease_seconds <= 0:
   490	            raise GatewayError("invalid_lease", "claim lease must be positive")
   491	        with self.store.transaction() as db:
   492	            actor = self._authorize(db, credential, "claim")
   493	            if actor.startswith("coordinator:"):
   494	                raise GatewayError("worker_required", "coordinator credentials cannot claim coding work")
   495	            card = self._card(db, card_id)
   496	            self._expected(card, expected_revision)
   497	            self._definition(card, expected_definition_hash)
   498	            if card["status"] != "ready":
   499	                raise GatewayError("card_not_ready", "only a Ready card can be claimed", card["revision"])
   500	            definition = json.loads(card["definition_json"])
   501	            namespace = actor.split(":", 1)[0]
   502	            if namespace not in definition["allowedOwnerNamespaces"]:
   503	                raise GatewayError("owner_namespace_denied", f"owner namespace {namespace} is not allowed")
   504	            active = db.execute("SELECT card_id FROM claims WHERE owner=? AND closed_at IS NULL", (actor,)).fetchone()
   505	            if active is not None:
   506	                raise GatewayError("wip_limit", f"owner already holds {active['card_id']}")
   507	            for dependency in self._dependencies(db, card_id):
   508	                dep = db.execute("SELECT status FROM cards WHERE card_id=?", (dependency,)).fetchone()
   509	                if dep is None or dep["status"] != "done":
   510	                    raise GatewayError("dependency_unmet", f"dependency {dependency} is not Done")
   511	            paths = self._paths(db, card_id)
   512	            reservations = db.execute("SELECT card_id,path FROM path_reservations WHERE card_id<>?", (card_id,)).fetchall()
   513	            for path in paths:
   514	                for reservation in reservations:
   515	                    if _overlaps(path, reservation["path"]):
   516	                        raise GatewayError("path_conflict", f"path {path} conflicts with card {reservation['card_id']}")
   517	            fence = card["fencing_generation"] + 1
   518	            claim_id, now = str(uuid4()), self._now()
   519	            db.execute("UPDATE cards SET status='claimed',owner=?,revision=revision+1,fencing_generation=?,attention_required=0,updated_at=? WHERE card_id=?", (actor, fence, now, card_id))
   520	            db.execute("INSERT INTO claims VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,NULL,NULL)", (claim_id, card_id, actor, fence, card["definition_hash"], now, now, now + lease_seconds))
   521	            updated = db.execute("UPDATE path_reservations SET fencing_token=? WHERE card_id=?", (fence, card_id)).rowcount
   522	            if updated != len(paths):
   523	                raise GatewayError("reservation_lost", "Ready path reservations are incomplete")
   524	            revision = card["revision"] + 1
   525	            claim_row = db.execute("SELECT * FROM claims WHERE claim_id=?", (claim_id,)).fetchone()
   675	        with self.store.read() as db:
   676	            submitted = db.execute("SELECT payload_json FROM receipts WHERE card_id=? AND kind='submit' ORDER BY receipt_id DESC LIMIT 1", (card_id,)).fetchone()
   677	            if submitted is None or json.loads(submitted["payload_json"]).get("head_commit") != review_head:
   678	                raise GatewayError("review_head_mismatch", "integration review head differs from immutable submit receipt")
   679	        result = self._coordinator_transition(scope="integrate", card_id=card_id, expected_revision=expected_revision, credential=credential, allowed={"review"}, target="verifying", kind="integrate", payload={"integrated_commit": integrated_commit, "review_head": review_head, "ancestry": dict(ancestry), "evidence": list(evidence)}, fencing_token=fencing_token)
   680	        return result
   681	
   682	    def accept(self, *, card_id: str, expected_revision: int, credential: str, fencing_token: int, evidence: Sequence[str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   683	        if not evidence:
   684	            raise GatewayError("evidence_required", "acceptance needs independent evidence")
   685	        return self._coordinator_transition(scope="accept", card_id=card_id, expected_revision=expected_revision, credential=credential, allowed={"verifying"}, target="done", kind="accept", payload={"evidence": list(evidence)}, close_claim=True, release_paths=True, fencing_token=fencing_token)
   686	
   687	    def cancel(self, *, card_id: str, expected_revision: int, credential: str, reason: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
   688	        if not reason: raise GatewayError("invalid_reason", "cancel reason must be non-empty")
   689	        return self._coordinator_transition(scope="cancel", card_id=card_id, expected_revision=expected_revision, credential=credential, allowed=set(ACTIVE_STATUSES) | {"ready", "backlog"}, target="cancelled", kind="cancel", payload={"reason": reason}, close_claim=True, release_paths=True)
   690	
   691	    def requeue(self, *, card_id: str, expected_revision: int, credential: str, reason: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
   692	        if not reason: raise GatewayError("invalid_reason", "requeue reason must be non-empty")
   693	        return self._coordinator_transition(scope="requeue", card_id=card_id, expected_revision=expected_revision, credential=credential, allowed=set(ACTIVE_STATUSES), target="ready", kind="requeue", payload={"reason": reason}, close_claim=True, release_paths=False)
   694	
   695	    def reassign(self, *, card_id: str, expected_revision: int, credential: str, new_owner: str, lease_seconds: int = 120, reason: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
   696	        if not new_owner or new_owner.startswith("coordinator:") or lease_seconds <= 0:
   697	            raise GatewayError("invalid_owner", "reassignment needs a worker owner and positive lease")
   698	        if not reason.strip():
   699	            raise GatewayError("invalid_reason", "reassignment reason must be non-empty")
   700	        with self.store.transaction() as db:
   701	            actor = self._authorize(db, credential, "reassign", coordinator=True)
   702	            card = self._card(db, card_id); self._expected(card, expected_revision)
   703	            if card["status"] not in ACTIVE_STATUSES:
   704	                raise GatewayError("invalid_transition", "only an active card can be reassigned", card["revision"])
   705	            if db.execute("SELECT 1 FROM claims WHERE card_id=? AND closed_at IS NULL", (card_id,)).fetchone() is None:
   706	                raise GatewayError("claim_not_active", "reassignment requires an active claim", card["revision"])
   707	            if db.execute("SELECT 1 FROM claims WHERE owner=? AND closed_at IS NULL", (new_owner,)).fetchone():
   708	                raise GatewayError("wip_limit", "new owner already has an active claim")
   709	            now = self._now(); fence = card["fencing_generation"] + 1; claim_id = str(uuid4()); revision = card["revision"] + 1
   710	            db.execute("UPDATE claims SET closed_at=?,close_reason='reassign' WHERE card_id=? AND closed_at IS NULL", (now, card_id))
   711	            db.execute("UPDATE cards SET status='claimed',owner=?,revision=?,fencing_generation=?,attention_required=0,updated_at=? WHERE card_id=?", (new_owner, revision, fence, now, card_id))
   712	            db.execute("INSERT INTO claims VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,?,?,NULL,NULL)", (claim_id, card_id, new_owner, fence, card["definition_hash"], now, now, now + lease_seconds))
   713	            if new_owner.split(":", 1)[0] not in json.loads(card["definition_json"])["allowedOwnerNamespaces"]:
   714	                raise GatewayError("owner_namespace_denied", "new owner namespace is not allowed")
   715	            paths = self._paths(db, card_id)
   716	            reservations = db.execute("SELECT card_id,path FROM path_reservations WHERE card_id<>?", (card_id,)).fetchall()
   717	            for path in paths:
   718	                for reservation in reservations:
   719	                    if _overlaps(path, reservation["path"]):
   720	                        raise GatewayError("path_conflict", f"path {path} conflicts with card {reservation['card_id']}")
   721	            db.execute("DELETE FROM path_reservations WHERE card_id=?", (card_id,))
   722	            db.executemany("INSERT INTO path_reservations(card_id,path,fencing_token) VALUES(?,?,?)", ((card_id, path, fence) for path in paths))
   723	            refreshed_card = self._card(db, card_id)
   724	            refreshed_claim = db.execute("SELECT * FROM claims WHERE claim_id=?", (claim_id,)).fetchone()
   725	            self._store_claim_bundle(db, refreshed_card, refreshed_claim)
   726	            receipt_hash = self._receipt(db, card_id=card_id, kind="reassign", actor=actor, revision_from=card["revision"], revision_to=revision, fencing_token=fence, payload={"new_owner": new_owner, "reason": reason, "claim_id": claim_id})
   727	            return {"card_id": card_id, "status": "claimed", "owner": new_owner, "claim_id": claim_id, "fencing_token": fence, "revision": revision, "expires_at": now + lease_seconds, "receipt_hash": receipt_hash}
   728	
   729	    def revalidate(self, *, card_id: str, expected_revision: int, credential: str, definition: Mapping[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   730	        new_hash = self._validate_definition_contract(definition)
   731	        with self.store.transaction() as db:
   732	            actor = self._authorize(db, credential, "revalidate", coordinator=True)
   733	            card = self._card(db, card_id); self._expected(card, expected_revision)
   734	            revision = card["revision"] + 1
   735	            claim = db.execute("SELECT * FROM claims WHERE card_id=? AND closed_at IS NULL", (card_id,)).fetchone()
   736	            fence = card["fencing_generation"]
   737	            if claim is not None:
   738	                if claim["owner"].split(":", 1)[0] not in definition["allowedOwnerNamespaces"]:
   739	                    raise GatewayError("owner_namespace_denied", "active owner is not allowed by revalidated definition")
   740	                fence += 1
   741	            db.execute("UPDATE cards SET definition_json=?,definition_hash=?,source_revision=?,revalidation_required=0,revision=?,fencing_generation=?,updated_at=? WHERE card_id=?", (_canonical(definition), new_hash, definition["sourceRevision"], revision, fence, self._now(), card_id))
   742	            task_bundle = None
   743	            if claim is not None:
   744	                db.execute("UPDATE claims SET definition_hash=?,fencing_token=? WHERE claim_id=?", (new_hash, fence, claim["claim_id"]))
   745	                db.execute("UPDATE path_reservations SET fencing_token=? WHERE card_id=?", (fence, card_id))
   746	                db.execute("UPDATE worktree_bindings SET fencing_token=? WHERE claim_id=?", (fence, claim["claim_id"]))
   747	                refreshed_card = self._card(db, card_id)
   748	                refreshed_claim = db.execute("SELECT * FROM claims WHERE claim_id=?", (claim["claim_id"],)).fetchone()
   749	                task_bundle = self._store_claim_bundle(db, refreshed_card, refreshed_claim)
   750	            receipt_hash = self._receipt(db, card_id=card_id, kind="revalidate", actor=actor, revision_from=card["revision"], revision_to=revision, fencing_token=fence or None, payload={"definition_hash": new_hash, "fencing_token": fence})
   751	            result = {"card_id": card_id, "status": card["status"], "revision": revision, "fencing_token": fence, "definition_hash": new_hash, "receipt_hash": receipt_hash}
   752	            if task_bundle is not None:
   753	                task_bundle["receipt_hash"] = receipt_hash
   754	                result["task_bundle"] = task_bundle
   755	            return result

   430	        credential=coordinator, new_owner=pi_owner, reason="move to pi seat",
   431	    )
   432	    assert reassigned["owner"] == pi_owner
   433	    assert next(
   434	        card for card in gateway.list_cards() if card["card_id"] == "PI-ALLOWED"
   435	    )["owner"] == pi_owner
   436	
   437	    restricted_definition = definition()
   438	    restricted_definition["allowedOwnerNamespaces"] = ["codex"]
   439	    restricted_definition["definitionHash"] = compute_definition_hash(restricted_definition)
   440	    restricted = gateway.qualify_card(
   441	        card_id="PI-DENIED", title="pi denied", paths=("pi-denied",),
   442	        definition=restricted_definition, credential=coordinator,
   443	        authority_grant=AUTHORITY_GRANT, repository_id=REPOSITORY_ID,
   444	    )
   445	    restricted_claim = gateway.claim(
   446	        card_id="PI-DENIED", expected_revision=restricted["revision"],
   447	        expected_definition_hash=restricted["definition_hash"], credential=host_a,
   448	    )
   449	
   450	    with pytest.raises(GatewayError) as denied:
   451	        gateway.reassign(
   452	            card_id="PI-DENIED", expected_revision=restricted_claim["revision"],
   453	            credential=coordinator, new_owner="pi:host-c:denied",
   454	            reason="attempt disallowed pi move",
   455	        )
   456	
   457	    assert denied.value.code == "owner_namespace_denied"
   458	    assert denied.value.message == "new owner namespace is not allowed"
   459	    denied_card = next(
   460	        card for card in gateway.list_cards() if card["card_id"] == "PI-DENIED"
   461	    )
   462	    assert denied_card["owner"] == "codex:host-a:seat"
   463	    assert denied_card["revision"] == restricted_claim["revision"]
   464	
   465	
   466	def test_checkpoint_requires_bound_exact_structured_lineage(setup):
   467	    gateway, _, coordinator, host_a, _ = setup
   468	    ready = qualify(gateway, coordinator)
   469	    gateway.claim(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=1, expected_definition_hash=ready["definition_hash"], credential=host_a)
   470	    ancestry = {"base_commit": "abc", "head_commit": "def", "is_descendant": True, "verification": "git merge-base --is-ancestor abc def"}
   471	    with pytest.raises(GatewayError) as before_bind:
   472	        gateway.checkpoint(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=2, fencing_token=1, credential=host_a, checkpoint="work", repository_id=REPOSITORY_ID, branch="dev/meta-2", base_commit="abc", head_commit="def", ancestry=ancestry)
   473	    assert before_bind.value.code == "invalid_transition"
   474	    with pytest.raises(GatewayError) as mismatch:
   475	        gateway.bind_worktree(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=2, fencing_token=1, credential=host_a, repository_id=REPOSITORY_ID, worktree_path="/wrong", branch="dev/meta-2", base_commit="abc")
   476	    assert mismatch.value.code == "lineage_mismatch"
   477	    gateway.bind_worktree(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=2, fencing_token=1, credential=host_a, repository_id=REPOSITORY_ID, worktree_path="/work/meta-2", branch="dev/meta-2", base_commit="abc")
   478	    invalid = {**ancestry, "is_descendant": False}
   479	    with pytest.raises(GatewayError) as bad_head:
   480	        gateway.checkpoint(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=3, fencing_token=1, credential=host_a, checkpoint="work", repository_id=REPOSITORY_ID, branch="dev/meta-2", base_commit="abc", head_commit="def", ancestry=invalid)
   481	    assert bad_head.value.code == "invalid_lineage"
   482	    checkpoint = gateway.checkpoint(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=3, fencing_token=1, credential=host_a, checkpoint="work", repository_id=REPOSITORY_ID, branch="dev/meta-2", base_commit="abc", head_commit="def", ancestry=ancestry)
   483	    assert checkpoint["revision"] == 4

   486	def test_integrate_enforces_frozen_review_head_live_fence_and_ancestry(setup):
   487	    gateway, _, coordinator, host_a, _ = setup
   488	    ready = qualify(gateway, coordinator)
   489	    gateway.claim(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=1, expected_definition_hash=ready["definition_hash"], credential=host_a)

   496	    assert wrong_head.value.code == "review_head_mismatch"
   497	    with pytest.raises(GatewayError) as stale:
   498	        gateway.integrate(card_id="META-2", expected_revision=submitted["revision"], credential=coordinator, fencing_token=0, integrated_commit="fed", review_head="def", ancestry=ancestry, evidence=("review",))
   499	    assert stale.value.code == "stale_fence"
   500	    with pytest.raises(GatewayError) as invalid:
   560	    assert reclaimed.id == item.id and reclaimed.attempts == item.attempts + 1

   119	function makeDefinition(overrides = {}, callerWorktree = "/tmp/worktree") {
   120	  const definition = { ...baseDefinition(callerWorktree), ...overrides };
   121	  definition.definitionHash = computeDefinitionHash(definition);
   122	  return definition;
   123	}
   124	
   125	async function writeDefinition(path, overrides = {}, callerWorktree = "/tmp/worktree") {
   126	  const definition = makeDefinition(overrides, callerWorktree);
   127	  await writeFile(path, `${JSON.stringify(definition, null, 2)}\n`);
   128	  return definition;
   129	}

   147	async function readyCard(root, id, overrides = {}, expectedRevision = "1") {
   148	  const definitionPath = join(root, "definition.json");
   149	  await writeDefinition(definitionPath, overrides, root);
   150	  const result = await run([
   151	    "ready",
   152	    id,
   153	    "--control-root",
   154	    root,
   155	    "--caller-worktree",
   156	    root,
   157	    "--expected-revision",
   158	    expectedRevision,
   159	    "--owner",
   160	    coordinatorOwner(),
   161	    "--definition-json",
   162	    definitionPath,
   163	  ]);
   164	  if (result.code !== 0) {
   165	    throw new Error(`ready failed: ${result.stderr}`);
   166	  }
   167	  return JSON.parse(result.stdout);
   168	}
   169	
   170	async function claimCard(root, id, owner, expectedRevision = "2") {
   171	  const result = await run([
   172	    "claim",
   173	    id,
   174	    "--control-root",
   175	    root,
   176	    "--caller-worktree",
   177	    root,
   178	    "--expected-revision",
   179	    expectedRevision,
   180	    "--owner",
   181	    owner,
   182	  ]);
   183	  if (result.code !== 0) {
   184	    throw new Error(`claim failed: ${result.stderr}`);
   185	  }
   186	  return JSON.parse(result.stdout);
   187	}

  3787	test("start transitions claimed card to in_progress and appends receipt", async (context) => {
  3788	  const { root, parent } = await repository(
  3789	    state([
  3790	      card({
  3791	        id: "TASK-20260711-001",
  3792	        title: "Startable",
  3793	        status: "backlog",
  3794	        owner: "",
  3795	        paths: ["src/start"],
  3796	      }),
  3797	    ]),
  3798	  );
  3799	  context.after(() => rm(parent, { recursive: true, force: true }));
  3800	
  3801	  const owner = codexOwner("start-session");
  3802	  await readyCard(root, "TASK-20260711-001");
  3803	  await claimCard(root, "TASK-20260711-001", owner);
  3804	
  3805	  const before = Date.now();
  3806	  const result = await run([
  3807	    "start",
  3808	    "TASK-20260711-001",
  3809	    "--control-root",
  3810	    root,
  3811	    "--caller-worktree",
  3812	    root,
  3813	    "--expected-revision",
  3814	    "3",
  3815	    "--owner",
  3816	    owner,
  3817	  ]);
  3818	  const after = Date.now();
  3819	  assert.equal(result.code, 0, result.stderr);
  3820	  const output = JSON.parse(result.stdout);
  3821	  assert.equal(output.revision, 4);
  3822	  assert.equal(output.started, true);
  3823	
  3824	  const finalState = JSON.parse(
  3825	    await readFile(join(root, ".workplan", "state.json"), "utf8"),
  3826	  );
  3827	  assert.equal(finalState.revision, 4);
  3828	  const startedCard = finalState.cards.find((c) => c.id === "TASK-20260711-001");
  3829	  assert.equal(startedCard.status, "in_progress");
  3830	  assert.equal(startedCard.owner, owner);
  3831	  assert.ok(startedCard.claimSnapshot);
  3832	  assert.ok(startedCard.definition);
  3833	  assert.deepEqual(startedCard.paths, ["src/start"]);
  3834	
  3835	  const startReceipt = startedCard.receipts[startedCard.receipts.length - 1];
  3836	  assert.equal(startReceipt.from, "claimed");
  3837	  assert.equal(startReceipt.to, "in_progress");
  3838	  assert.equal(startReceipt.actor, owner);
  3839	  assert.equal(startReceipt.revisionFrom, 3);
  3840	  assert.equal(startReceipt.revisionTo, 4);
  3841	  const at = new Date(startReceipt.at).getTime();
  3842	  assert.ok(at >= before && at <= after);
  3843	
  3844	  const projection = await readFile(join(root, "WORKPLAN.md"), "utf8");
  3845	  assert.match(projection, /TASK-20260711-001/);
  3846	  assert.match(projection, /in_progress/);
  3847	  assert.match(projection, /start-session/);
  3848	});

  3853	      card({

  3868	  await seedCommit(root);
  3869

  3904	  assert.equal(submittedCard.reviewFreeze.revisionFrom, 4);
  3905	  assert.equal(submittedCard.reviewFreeze.revisionTo, 5);
  3906	  const freezeAt = new Date(submittedCard.reviewFreeze.at).getTime();
  3907	  assert.ok(freezeAt >= before && freezeAt <= after);
  3908

  3910	  assert.equal(submitReceipt.from, "in_progress");
  3911	  assert.equal(submitReceipt.to, "review");
  3912	  assert.equal(submitReceipt.actor, owner);

  3914	  assert.equal(submitReceipt.revisionTo, 5);
  3915	  assert.equal(submitReceipt.evidence.head, head);
  3916	  assert.equal(submitReceipt.evidence.branch, "main");

  1316	async function claim(options) {
  1317	  const { controlRoot, callerWorktree, expectedRevision, id, owner } = options;
  1318	
  1319	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  1320	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  1321	  }
  1322	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  1323	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  1324	  }
  1325	
  1326	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  1327	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  1328	
  1329	  const acquired = await acquireClaimLock(controlRoot);
  1330	  try {
  1331	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  1332	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  1333	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  1334	    validateState(state);
  1335	
  1336	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  1337	      fail(
  1338	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  1339	      );
  1340	    }
  1341	
  1342	    const card = state.cards.find((c) => c.id === id);
  1343	    if (!card) {
  1344	      fail(`card ${id} not found`);
  1345	    }
  1346	
  1347	    validateClaimCandidateBasics(card, callerWorktree);
  1348	    validateClaimEligibility(card, owner, state);
  1349	
  1350	    const snapshot = makeClaimSnapshot(
  1351	      card,
  1352	      owner,
  1353	      expectedRevision,
  1354	      expectedRevision + 1,
  1355	    );
  1356	    card.status = "claimed";
  1357	    card.owner = owner;
  1358	    card.claimSnapshot = snapshot;
  1359	    appendReceipt(
  1360	      card,
  1361	      "ready",
  1362	      "claimed",
  1363	      owner,
  1364	      expectedRevision,
  1365	      expectedRevision + 1,
  1366	    );
  1367	
  1368	    state.revision += 1;
  1369	
  1370	    const workplanPath = join(controlRoot, "WORKPLAN.md");
  1371	    const tempMd = join(controlRoot, `WORKPLAN.md.tmp-${process.pid}`);
  1372	    await writeFile(tempMd, renderWorkplan(state));
  1373	    await rename(tempMd, workplanPath);
  1374	
  1375	    if (process.env.WORKPLAN_FAULT_AFTER_PROJECTION === "1") {
  1376	      fail("injected fault after projection");
  1377	    }
  1378	
  1379	    const tempState = join(
  1380	      controlRoot,
  1381	      ".workplan",
  1382	      `state.json.tmp-${process.pid}`,
  1383	    );
  1384	    await writeFile(tempState, `${JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)}\n`);
  1385	    await rename(tempState, statePath);
  1386	
  1387	    return { revision: state.revision, claimed: true };
  1388	  } finally {
  1389	    await releaseClaimLock(acquired);
  1390	  }
  1391	}

  1393	function sortClaimNextCandidates(candidates) {
  1394	  return candidates.sort((a, b) => {
  1395	    const aHas = a.priority !== undefined;
  1396	    const bHas = b.priority !== undefined;
  1397	    if (aHas && bHas) {
  1398	      if (a.priority !== b.priority) return a.priority - b.priority;
  1399	      return a.id.localeCompare(b.id);
  1400	    }
  1401	    if (aHas && !bHas) return -1;
  1402	    if (!aHas && bHas) return 1;
  1403	    return a.id.localeCompare(b.id);
  1404	  });
  1405	}

  1407	async function claimNext(options) {
  1408	  const { controlRoot, callerWorktree, expectedRevision, owner } = options;
  1409	
  1410	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  1411	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  1412	  }
  1413	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  1414	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  1415	  }
  1416	
  1417	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  1418	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  1419	
  1420	  const acquired = await acquireClaimLock(controlRoot);
  1421	  try {
  1422	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  1423	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  1424	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  1425	    validateState(state);
  1426	
  1427	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  1428	      fail(
  1429	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  1430	      );
  1431	    }
  1432	
  1433	    const readyCards = state.cards.filter((c) => c.status === "ready");
  1434	    for (const candidate of readyCards) {
  1435	      validateClaimCandidateBasics(candidate, callerWorktree);
  1436	    }
  1437	    const candidates = sortClaimNextCandidates(readyCards);
  1438	
  1439	    for (const candidate of candidates) {
  1440	      try {
  1441	        validateClaimEligibility(candidate, owner, state);
  1442	      } catch (error) {
  1443	        if (!error.isExpected) throw error;
  1444	        continue;
  1445	      }
  1446	
  1447	      const snapshot = makeClaimSnapshot(
  1448	        candidate,
  1449	        owner,
  1450	        expectedRevision,
  1451	        expectedRevision + 1,
  1452	      );
  1453	      candidate.status = "claimed";
  1454	      candidate.owner = owner;
  1455	      candidate.claimSnapshot = snapshot;
  1456	      appendReceipt(
  1457	        candidate,
  1458	        "ready",
  1459	        "claimed",
  1460	        owner,
  1461	        expectedRevision,
  1462	        expectedRevision + 1,
  1463	      );
  1464	
  1465	      state.revision += 1;
  1720	    execFile(
  1721	      "git",
  1722	      ["-C", dir, "rev-parse", "--abbrev-ref", "HEAD"],
  1723	      { timeout: 10000 },
  1724	      (error, stdout, stderr) => {
  1725	        if (error) {
  1726	          reject(
  1727	            new Error(
  1728	              `git branch unavailable for ${dir}: ${stderr || error.message}`,
  1729	            ),
  1730	          );
  1731	          return;
  1732	        }
  1733	        const branch = stdout.trim();
  1734	        execFile(
  1735	          "git",
  1736	          ["-C", dir, "rev-parse", "HEAD"],
  1737	          { timeout: 10000 },
  1738	          (error2, stdout2, stderr2) => {
  1739	            if (error2) {
  1740	              reject(
  1741	                new Error(
  1742	                  `git HEAD unavailable for ${dir}: ${stderr2 || error2.message}`,
  1743	                ),
  1744	              );
  1745	              return;
  1746	            }
  1747	            resolve({ branch, head: stdout2.trim() });
  1748	          },
  1749	        );
  1750	      },
  1751	    );
  1752	  });
  1753	}

  1755	async function start(options) {
  1756	  const { controlRoot, callerWorktree, expectedRevision, id, owner } = options;
  1757	
  1758	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  1759	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  1760	  }
  1761	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  1762	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  1763	  }
  1764	
  1765	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  1766	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  1767	
  1768	  const acquired = await acquireTransitionLock(controlRoot);
  1769	  try {
  1770	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  1771	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  1772	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  1773	    validateState(state);
  1774	
  1775	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  1776	      fail(
  1777	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  1778	      );
  1779	    }
  1780	
  1781	    const card = state.cards.find((c) => c.id === id);
  1782	    if (!card) {
  1783	      fail(`card ${id} not found`);
  1784	    }
  1785	
  1786	    validateTransitionCard(card, owner, callerWorktree, "claimed");
  1787	
  1788	    appendReceipt(
  1789	      card,
  1790	      "claimed",
  1791	      "in_progress",
  1792	      owner,
  1793	      expectedRevision,
  1794	      expectedRevision + 1,
  1795	    );
  1796	    card.status = "in_progress";
  1797	
  1798	    state.revision += 1;
  1799	
  1800	    const workplanPath = join(controlRoot, "WORKPLAN.md");
  1801	    const tempMd = join(controlRoot, `WORKPLAN.md.tmp-${process.pid}`);
  1802	    await writeFile(tempMd, renderWorkplan(state));
  1803	    await rename(tempMd, workplanPath);
  1804	
  1805	    if (process.env.WORKPLAN_FAULT_AFTER_PROJECTION === "1") {
  1806	      fail("injected fault after projection");
  1807	    }
  1808	
  1809	    const tempState = join(
  1810	      controlRoot,
  1811	      ".workplan",
  1812	      `state.json.tmp-${process.pid}`,
  1813	    );
  1814	    await writeFile(tempState, `${JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)}\n`);
  1815	    await rename(tempState, statePath);
  1816	
  1817	    return { revision: state.revision, started: true };
  1818	  } finally {
  1819	    await releaseTransitionLock(acquired);
  1820	  }
  1821	}

  1823	async function submit(options) {
  1824	  const {
  1825	    controlRoot,
  1826	    callerWorktree,
  1827	    expectedRevision,
  1828	    id,
  1829	    owner,
  1830	    expectedHead,
  1831	  } = options;
  1832	
  1833	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  1834	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  1835	  }
  1836	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  1837	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  1838	  }
  1839	
  1840	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  1841	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  1842	
  1843	  const acquired = await acquireTransitionLock(controlRoot);
  1844	  try {
  1845	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  1846	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  1847	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  1848	    validateState(state);
  1849	
  1850	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  1851	      fail(
  1852	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  1853	      );
  1854	    }
  1855	
  1856	    const card = state.cards.find((c) => c.id === id);
  1857	    if (!card) {
  1858	      fail(`card ${id} not found`);
  1859	    }
  1860	
  1861	    validateTransitionCard(card, owner, callerWorktree, "in_progress");
  1862	
  1863	    const { branch, head } = await readGitBranchAndHead(callerWorktree);
  1864	    if (head !== expectedHead) {
  1865	      fail(`HEAD ${head} does not match expected ${expectedHead}`);
  1866	    }
  1867	
  1868	    card.reviewFreeze = {
  1869	      branch,
  1870	      head,

  1872	      revisionTo: expectedRevision + 1,
  1873	      at: new Date().toISOString(),
  1874	    };
  1875	    appendReceipt(
  2380	  }
  2381	  if (
  2382	    !receipt.evidence ||
  2383	    typeof receipt.evidence !== "object" ||
  2384	    Array.isArray(receipt.evidence)
  2385	  ) {
  2386	    fail("blocked receipt evidence missing");
  2387	  }

  2389	  if (
  2390	    evidenceKeys.length !== 2 ||

  2392	  ) {

  2394	  }

  2396	    typeof receipt.evidence.reason !== "string" ||
  2397	    receipt.evidence.reason.trim().length === 0
  2398	  ) {
  2399	    fail("blocked receipt evidence reason must be non-empty");
  2400	  }
  2401	  if (receipt.evidence.reason !== card.blockReason) {
  2402	    fail("blocked receipt evidence reason mismatch");
  2403	  }
  2404	  if (receipt.evidence.retainPaths !== card.retainPaths) {
  2405	    fail("blocked receipt evidence retainPaths mismatch");
  2406	  }
  2407	}

  2409	async function block(options) {
  2410	  const {
  2411	    controlRoot,
  2412	    callerWorktree,
  2413	    expectedRevision,
  2414	    id,
  2415	    owner,
  2416	    reason,
  2417	    retainPaths,
  2418	  } = options;
  2419	
  2420	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  2421	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  2422	  }
  2423	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  2424	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  2425	  }
  2426	  if (typeof reason !== "string" || reason.trim().length === 0) {
  2427	    fail("--reason must be a non-empty string");
  2428	  }
  2429	  if (typeof retainPaths !== "boolean") {
  2430	    fail("--retain-paths must be true or false");
  2431	  }
  2432	
  2433	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  2434	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  2435	
  2436	  const acquired = await acquireTransitionLock(controlRoot);
  2437	  try {
  2438	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  2439	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  2440	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  2441	    validateState(state);
  2442	
  2443	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  2444	      fail(
  2445	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  2446	      );
  2447	    }
  2448	
  2449	    const card = state.cards.find((c) => c.id === id);
  2450	    if (!card) {
  2451	      fail(`card ${id} not found`);
  2452	    }
  2453	    if (!BLOCKABLE_STATUSES.includes(card.status)) {
  2454	      fail(`card ${card.id} cannot be blocked from ${card.status} status`);
  2455	    }
  2456	    if (card.owner !== owner) {
  2457	      fail(`card ${card.id} is not owned by ${owner}`);
  2458	    }
  2459	
  2460	    validateTransitionCardBasics(card, card.status);
  2461	    if (card.definition.worktreePath !== callerWorktree) {
  2462	      fail("worktreePath must match callerWorktree");
  2463	    }
  2464	    if (["review", "verifying"].includes(card.status)) {
  2465	      validateReviewFreeze(card);
  2466	    }
  2467	    if (card.status === "verifying") {
  2468	      validateIntegrationReceipt(card, expectedRevision);
  2469	    }
  2470	
  2471	    card.blockedFrom = card.status;
  2472	    card.blockReason = reason;
  2473	    card.retainPaths = retainPaths;
  2474	    card.status = "blocked";
  2475	
  2476	    appendReceipt(
  2477	      card,
  2478	      card.blockedFrom,
  2479	      "blocked",
  2480	      owner,
  2481	      expectedRevision,
  2482	      expectedRevision + 1,
  2483	      { reason, retainPaths },
  2484	    );
  2485	
  2486	    state.revision += 1;
  2487	
  2488	    const workplanPath = join(controlRoot, "WORKPLAN.md");
  2489	    const tempMd = join(controlRoot, `WORKPLAN.md.tmp-${process.pid}`);
  2490	    await writeFile(tempMd, renderWorkplan(state));
  2491	    await rename(tempMd, workplanPath);
  2492	
  2493	    if (process.env.WORKPLAN_FAULT_AFTER_PROJECTION === "1") {
  2494	      fail("injected fault after projection");
  2495	    }
  2496	
  2497	    const tempState = join(
  2498	      controlRoot,
  2499	      ".workplan",
  2500	      `state.json.tmp-${process.pid}`,
  2501	    );
  2502	    await writeFile(tempState, `${JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)}\n`);
  2503	    await rename(tempState, statePath);
  2504	
  2505	    return { revision: state.revision, blocked: true };
  2506	  } finally {
  2507	    await releaseTransitionLock(acquired);
  2508	  }
  2509	}
  2510	
  2511	async function resume(options) {
  2512	  const { controlRoot, callerWorktree, expectedRevision, id, owner } = options;
  2513	
  2514	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  2515	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  2516	  }

  1293	  card,
  1294	  from,
  1295	  to,
  1296	  actor,
  1297	  revisionFrom,
  1298	  revisionTo,
  1299	  evidence,
  1300	) {
  1301	  card.receipts = [...(card.receipts || [])];

  1309	  };
  1310	  if (evidence !== undefined) {
  1311	    receipt.evidence = evidence;
  1312	  }
  1313	  card.receipts.push(receipt);
  1314	}

  1316	async function claim(options) {
  1317	  const { controlRoot, callerWorktree, expectedRevision, id, owner } = options;
  1318	
  1319	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  1320	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  1321	  }
  1322	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  1323	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  1324	  }
  1325	
  1326	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  1327	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  1328	
  1329	  const acquired = await acquireClaimLock(controlRoot);
  1330	  try {
  1331	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  1332	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  1333	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  1334	    validateState(state);
  1335	
  1336	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  1337	      fail(
  1338	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  1339	      );
  1340	    }
  1341	
  1342	    const card = state.cards.find((c) => c.id === id);
  1343	    if (!card) {
  1344	      fail(`card ${id} not found`);
  1345	    }
  1346	
  1347	    validateClaimCandidateBasics(card, callerWorktree);
  1348	    validateClaimEligibility(card, owner, state);
  1349	
  1350	    const snapshot = makeClaimSnapshot(
  1351	      card,
  1352	      owner,
  1353	      expectedRevision,
  1354	      expectedRevision + 1,
  1355	    );
  1356	    card.status = "claimed";
  1357	    card.owner = owner;
  1358	    card.claimSnapshot = snapshot;
  1359	    appendReceipt(
  1360	      card,
  1361	      "ready",
  1362	      "claimed",
  1363	      owner,
  1364	      expectedRevision,
  1365	      expectedRevision + 1,
  1366	    );
  1367	
  1368	    state.revision += 1;
  1369	
  1370	    const workplanPath = join(controlRoot, "WORKPLAN.md");
  1371	    const tempMd = join(controlRoot, `WORKPLAN.md.tmp-${process.pid}`);
  1372	    await writeFile(tempMd, renderWorkplan(state));
  1373	    await rename(tempMd, workplanPath);
  1374	
  1375	    if (process.env.WORKPLAN_FAULT_AFTER_PROJECTION === "1") {
  1376	      fail("injected fault after projection");
  1377	    }
  1378	
  1379	    const tempState = join(
  1380	      controlRoot,
  1381	      ".workplan",
  1382	      `state.json.tmp-${process.pid}`,
  1383	    );
  1384	    await writeFile(tempState, `${JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)}\n`);
  1385	    await rename(tempState, statePath);
  1386	
  1387	    return { revision: state.revision, claimed: true };
  1388	  } finally {
  1389	    await releaseClaimLock(acquired);
  1390	  }
  1391	}

  1393	function sortClaimNextCandidates(candidates) {
  1394	  return candidates.sort((a, b) => {
  1395	    const aHas = a.priority !== undefined;
  1396	    const bHas = b.priority !== undefined;
  1397	    if (aHas && bHas) {
  1398	      if (a.priority !== b.priority) return a.priority - b.priority;
  1399	      return a.id.localeCompare(b.id);
  1400	    }
  1401	    if (aHas && !bHas) return -1;
  1402	    if (!aHas && bHas) return 1;
  1403	    return a.id.localeCompare(b.id);
  1404	  });
  1405	}

  1407	async function claimNext(options) {
  1408	  const { controlRoot, callerWorktree, expectedRevision, owner } = options;
  1409	
  1410	  if (!isAbsolute(controlRoot)) {
  1411	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  1412	  }
  1413	  if (!isAbsolute(callerWorktree)) {
  1414	    fail("--caller-worktree must be an absolute path");
  1415	  }
  1416	
  1417	  parseClaimOwner(owner);
  1418	  await assertSameRepository(controlRoot, callerWorktree);
  1419	
  1420	  const acquired = await acquireClaimLock(controlRoot);
  1421	  try {
  1422	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  1423	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  1424	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  1425	    validateState(state);
  1426	
  1427	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  1428	      fail(
  1429	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  1430	      );
  1431	    }
  1432	
  1433	    const readyCards = state.cards.filter((c) => c.status === "ready");
  1434	    for (const candidate of readyCards) {
  1435	      validateClaimCandidateBasics(candidate, callerWorktree);
  1436	    }
  1437	    const candidates = sortClaimNextCandidates(readyCards);
  1438	
  1439	    for (const candidate of candidates) {
  1440	      try {
  1441	        validateClaimEligibility(candidate, owner, state);
  1442	      } catch (error) {
  1443	        if (!error.isExpected) throw error;
  1444	        continue;
  1445	      }
  1446	
  1447	      const snapshot = makeClaimSnapshot(
  1448	        candidate,
  1449	        owner,
  1450	        expectedRevision,
  1451	        expectedRevision + 1,
  1452	      );
  1453	      candidate.status = "claimed";
  1454	      candidate.owner = owner;
  1455	      candidate.claimSnapshot = snapshot;
  1456	      appendReceipt(
  1457	        candidate,
  1458	        "ready",
  1459	        "claimed",
  1460	        owner,
  1461	        expectedRevision,
  1462	        expectedRevision + 1,
  1463	      );
  1464	
  1465	      state.revision += 1;
  1720	    execFile(
  1721	      "git",
  1722	      ["-C", dir, "rev-parse", "--abbrev-ref", "HEAD"],
  1723	      { timeout: 10000 },
  1724	      (error, stdout, stderr) => {
  1725	        if (error) {
  1726	          reject(
  1727	            new Error(
  1728	              `git branch unavailable for ${dir}: ${stderr || error.message}`,
  1729	            ),
  1730	          );
  1731	          return;
  1732	        }
  1733	        const branch = stdout.trim();
  1734	        execFile(
  1735	          "git",
  1736	          ["-C", dir, "rev-parse", "HEAD"],
  1737	          { timeout: 10000 },
  1738	          (error2, stdout2, stderr2) => {
  1739	            if (error2) {
  1740	              reject(
  1741	                new Error(
  1742	                  `git HEAD unavailable for ${dir}: ${stderr2 || error2.message}`,
  1743	                ),
  1744	              );
  1745	              return;
  1746	            }
  1747	            resolve({ branch, head: stdout2.trim() });
  1748	          },
  1749	        );
  1750	      },
  1751	    );
  1752	  });
  1753	}

  2409	async function block(options) {

  2421	    fail("--control-root must be an absolute path");
  2422	  }

  2432	
  2433	  parseClaimOwner(owner);

  2435	
  2436	  const acquired = await acquireTransitionLock(controlRoot);
  2437	  try {
  2438	    const statePath = join(controlRoot, ".workplan", "state.json");
  2439	    const raw = await readFile(statePath, "utf8");
  2440	    const state = JSON.parse(raw);
  2441	    validateState(state);
  2442	
  2443	    if (state.revision !== expectedRevision) {
  2444	      fail(
  2445	        `expected revision ${expectedRevision} but found ${state.revision}`,
  2446	      );
  2447	    }
  2448	
  2449	    const card = state.cards.find((c) => c.id === id);

  2451	      fail(`card ${id} not found`);
  2452	    }

  2454	      fail(`card ${card.id} cannot be blocked from ${card.status} status`);
  2455	    }
  2456	    if (card.owner !== owner) {
  2457	      fail(`card ${card.id} is not owned by ${owner}`);
  2458	    }
  2459	
  2460	    validateTransitionCardBasics(card, card.status);
  2461	    if (card.definition.worktreePath !== callerWorktree) {
  2462	      fail("worktreePath must match callerWorktree");
  2463	    }
  2464	    if (["review", "verifying"].includes(card.status)) {
  2465	      validateReviewFreeze(card);
  2466	    }
  2467	    if (card.status === "verifying") {
  2468	      validateIntegrationReceipt(card, expectedRevision);
  2469	    }
  2470	
  2471	    card.blockedFrom = card.status;
  2472	    card.blockReason = reason;
  2473	    card.retainPaths = retainPaths;
  2474	    card.status = "blocked";
  2475	
  2476	    appendReceipt(
  2477	      card,
  2478	      card.blockedFrom,
  2479	      "blocked",
  2480	      owner,
  2481	      expectedRevision,
  2482	      expectedRevision + 1,
  2483	      { reason, retainPaths },
  2484	    );
  2485	
  2486	    state.revision += 1;
  2487	
  2488	    const workplanPath = join(controlRoot, "WORKPLAN.md");
  2489	    const tempMd = join(controlRoot, `WORKPLAN.md.tmp-${process.pid}`);
  2490	    await writeFile(tempMd, renderWorkplan(state));
  2491	    await rename(tempMd, workplanPath);
  2492	
  2493	    if (process.env.WORKPLAN_FAULT_AFTER_PROJECTION === "1") {
  2494	      fail("injected fault after projection");
  2495	    }
  2496	
  2497	    const tempState = join(
  2498	      controlRoot,
  2499	      ".workplan",
  2500	      `state.json.tmp-${process.pid}`,
  2501	    );
  2502	    await writeFile(tempState, `${JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)}\n`);
  2503	    await rename(tempState, statePath);
  2504	
  2505	    return { revision: state.revision, blocked: true };
  2506	  } finally {
  2507	    await releaseTransitionLock(acquired);
  2508	  }
  2509	}

  1229	function validateClaimPathExclusivity(card, state) {
  1230	  for (const other of state.cards) {
  1231	    if (other.id === card.id) continue;
  1232	    if (!isPathReserving(other)) continue;
  1233	    for (const path of card.paths) {

  1236	          fail(

  1238	          );
  1239	        }
  1240	      }
  1241	    }
  1242	  }
  1243	}

  1245	function validateNoOwnerWip(owner, card, state) {

It does not exercise the pi owner against the guard at [gateway.py:738](/private/tmp/meta-harness-t021/development/remote_workplan/gateway.py:738).
